style="text-align:right;font-size:115%;padding-top: 0.6em;padding-top:0"><div class="plainlinks hlist navbar mini"><ul><li class="nv-view"><a href="/wiki/Template:Formula_One" title="Template:Formula One"><abbr title="View this template">v</abbr></a></li><li class="nv-talk"><a href="/wiki/Template_talk:Formula_One" title="Template talk:Formula One"><abbr title="Discuss this template">t</abbr></a></li><li class="nv-edit"><a class="external text" href="//en.wikipedia.org/w/index.php?title=Template:Formula_One&amp;action=edit"><abbr title="Edit this template">e</abbr></a></li></ul></div></td></tr></tbody></table>\n<p>The <b>Formula One World Drivers\' Championship (WDC)</b> is awarded by the <a href="/wiki/F%C3%A9d%C3%A9ration_Internationale_de_l%27Automobile" title="F\xc3\xa9d\xc3\xa9ration Internationale de l&#39;Automobile">F\xc3\xa9d\xc3\xa9ration Internationale de l\'Automobile</a> (FIA) to the most successful <a href="/wiki/Formula_One" title="Formula One">Formula One</a> <a href="/wiki/Auto_racing" title="Auto racing">racing car driver</a> over a season, as determined by a <a href="/wiki/List_of_Formula_One_World_Championship_points_scoring_systems" title="List of Formula One World Championship points scoring systems">points system</a> based on individual <a href="/wiki/List_of_Formula_One_Grands_Prix" title="List of Formula One Grands Prix">Grand Prix</a> results.\n</p><p>The Drivers\' Championship was first awarded in <a href="/wiki/1950_Formula_One_season" title="1950 Formula One season">1950</a>, to <a href="/wiki/Giuseppe_Farina" title="Giuseppe Farina">Giuseppe Farina</a>. The first driver to win multiple Championships was <a href="/wiki/Alberto_Ascari" title="Alberto Ascari">Alberto Ascari</a>, in <a href="/wiki/1952_Formula_One_season" title="1952 Formula One season">1952</a> and <a href="/wiki/1953_Formula_One_season" title="1953 Formula One season">1953</a>. The current Drivers\' Champion is <a href="/wiki/Lewis_Hamilton" title="Lewis Hamilton">Lewis Hamilton</a> who won the World Championship in 2017.\n</p><p>A driver secures the World Championship each season (although it is not officially awarded until after the end of the season) as soon as it is no longer mathematically possible for another driver to beat him no matter what the outcome of the remaining races is. The Drivers\' Championship has been won in the final race of the season 29 times in the 68 seasons it has been awarded. The earliest in a season that the Drivers\' Championship has been clinched was in <a href="/wiki/2002_Formula_One_World_Championship" title="2002 Formula One World Championship">2002</a>, when Michael Schumacher secured the title with six races remaining.\n</p><p>Overall, thirty-three different drivers have won the Championship, with German Michael Schumacher holding the record for most titles, at seven. Schumacher also holds the record for most consecutive Drivers\' Championships, winning five from <a href="/wiki/2000_Formula_One_World_Championship" title="2000 Formula One World Championship">2000</a> to <a href="/wiki/2004_Formula_One_World_Championship" title="2004 Formula One World Championship">2004</a>. The <a href="/wiki/United_Kingdom" title="United Kingdom">United Kingdom</a> has produced the most World Championship winning drivers with ten; <a href="/wiki/Brazil" title="Brazil">Brazil</a>, <a href="/wiki/Germany" title="Germany">Germany</a> and <a href="/wiki/Finland" title="Finland">Finland</a> are next with three each. Of the 33 drivers to win the World Championship, twenty are still alive. The most recently deceased is <a href="/wiki/John_Surtees" title="John Surtees">John Surtees</a> (1934\xe2\x80\x932017). Among teams, <a href="/wiki/Scuderia_Ferrari" title="Scuderia Ferrari">Scuderia Ferrari</a> has produced the most World Championship winning drivers with 15.\n</p>\n<div id="toc" class="toc"><input id="Notes">Notes</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=List_of_Formula_One_World_Drivers%27_Champions&amp;action=edit&amp;section=2" title="Edit section: Notes">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>\n<p><b>Bold</b> indicates the team also won the <a href="/wiki/List_of_Formula_One_World_Constructors%27_Champions" title="List of Formula One World Constructors&#39; Champions">Constructors\' Championship</a> (awarded since <a href="/wiki/1958_Formula_One_season" title="1958 Formula One season">1958</a>).\n</p>\n<ol><li><span class="citation wikicite" id="endnote_d1"><b><a href="#ref_d1">^</a></b></span>  The <a href="/wiki/1952_Formula_One_season" title="1952 Formula One season">1952</a> and <a href="/wiki/1953_Formula_One_season" title="1953 Formula One season">1953</a> championships were run to <a href="/wiki/Formula_Two" title="Formula Two">Formula Two</a> regulations.</li>\n<li><span class="citation wikicite" id="endnote_d2"><b><a href="#ref_d2">^</a></b></span>  Fangio competed in the 1954 <a href="/wiki/1954_Argentine_Grand_Prix" title="1954 Argentine Grand Prix">Argentine</a> and <a href="/wiki/1954_Belgian_Grand_Prix" title="1954 Belgian Grand Prix">Belgian</a> Grands Prix with <a href="/wiki/Maserati_in_motorsport" title="Maserati in motorsport">Maserati</a>, then completed the season with <a href="/wiki/Mercedes-Benz_in_Formula_One" title="Mercedes-Benz in Formula One">Mercedes</a>.</li>\n<li><span class="citation wikicite" id="endnote_d3"><b><a href="#ref_d3">^</a></b></span>  Rindt\'s championship was confirmed two rounds after he had been killed in an accident during qualifying for the <a href="/wiki/1970_Italian_Grand_Prix" title="1970 Italian Grand Prix">Italian Grand Prix</a>.</li>\n<li><span class="citation wikicite" id="endnote_d4"><b><a href="#ref_d4">^</a></b></span>  <a href="/wiki/Michael_Schumacher" title="Michael Schumacher">Michael Schumacher</a> scored 78 points during the <a href="/wiki/1997_Formula_One_World_Championship" title="1997 Formula One World Championship">1997</a> season, 3 points behind Villeneuve, but was disqualified from the championship for deliberately colliding with Villeneuve in the final race of the season, the <a href="/wiki/1997_European_Grand_Prix" title="1997 European Grand Prix">European Grand Prix</a>. This left Villeneuve with a 39-point margin over <a href="/wiki/Heinz-Harald_Frentzen" title="Heinz-Harald Frentzen">Heinz-Harald Frentzen</a> with 42 points.</li></ol>\n<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="By_driver">By driver</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=List_of_Formula_One_World_Drivers%27_Champions&amp;action=edit&amp;section=3" title="Edit section: By driver">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>\n<div class="thumb tright"><div class="thumbinner" style="width:222px;"><a href="/wiki/File:Schumacher_(Ferrari)_in_practice_at_USGP_2005.jpg" class="image"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/9/9d/Schumacher_%28Ferrari%29_in_practice_at_USGP_2005.jpg/220px-Schumacher_%28Ferrari%29_in_practice_at_USGP_2005.jpg" width="220" height="86" class="thumbimage" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/9/9d/Schumacher_%28Ferrari%29_in_practice_at_USGP_2005.jpg/330px-Schumacher_%28Ferrari%29_in_practice_at_USGP_2005.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/9/9d/Schumacher_%28Ferrari%29_in_practice_at_USGP_2005.jpg/440px-Schumacher_%28Ferrari%29_in_practice_at_USGP_2005.jpg 2x" data-file-width="1798" data-file-height="700" /></a>  <div class="thumbcaption"><div class="magnify"><a href="/wiki/File:Schumacher_(Ferrari)_in_practice_at_USGP_2005.jpg" class="internal" title="Enlarge"></a></div><a href="/wiki/Michael_Schumacher" title="Michael Schumacher">Michael Schumacher</a> has won the World Drivers\' Championship a record seven times&#160;\xe2\x80\x93 twice with Benetton and five times with Ferrari. Five titles with a single team is also a record.</div></div></div>\n<div class="thumb tright"><div class="thumbinner" style="width:222px;"><a href="/wiki/File:Fangio-MB-W196-3lMotor-1986.jpg" class="image"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/a/a6/Fangio-MB-W196-3lMotor-1986.jpg/220px-Fangio-MB-W196-3lMotor-1986.jpg" width="220" height="172" class="thumbimage" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/a/a6/Fangio-MB-W196-3lMotor-1986.jpg/330px-Fangio-MB-W196-3lMotor-1986.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/a/a6/Fangio-MB-W196-3lMotor-1986.jpg/440px-Fangio-MB-W196-3lMotor-1986.jpg 2x" data-file-width="986" data-file-height="771" /></a>  <div class="thumbcaption"><div class="magnify"><a href="/wiki/File:Fangio-MB-W196-3lMotor-1986.jpg" class="internal" title="Enlarge"></a></div><a href="/wiki/Juan_Manuel_Fangio" title="Juan Manuel Fangio">Juan Manuel Fangio</a> won the World Drivers\' Championship five times with Alfa Romeo, Maserati, Mercedes and Ferrari. He held the record from 1955 until 2003.</div></div></div>\n<div class="thumb tright"><div class="thumbinner" style="width:222px;"><a href="/wiki/File:Alain_Prost_1988_Canada_2.jpg" class="image"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/9/91/Alain_Prost_1988_Canada_2.jpg/220px-Alain_Prost_1988_Canada_2.jpg" width="220" height="88" class="thumbimage" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/9/91/Alain_Prost_1988_Canada_2.jpg/330px-Alain_Prost_1988_Canada_2.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/9/91/Alain_Prost_1988_Canada_2.jpg/440px-Alain_Prost_1988_Canada_2.jpg 2x" data-file-width="612" data-file-height="245" /></a>  <div class="thumbcaption"><div class="magnify"><a href="/wiki/File:Alain_Prost_1988_Canada_2.jpg" class="internal" title="Enlarge"></a></div><a href="/wiki/Alain_Prost" title="Alain Prost">Alain Prost</a> has four titles, three for McLaren and one for Williams. He also came close to winning the title for Renault and for Ferrari.</div></div></div>\n<div class="thumb tright"><div class="thumbinner" style="width:222px;"><a href="/wiki/File:Sebastian_Vettel_2011_Malaysia_FP2_1.jpg" class="image"><img alt="" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/f/f7/Sebastian_Vettel_2011_Malaysia_FP2_1.jpg/330px-Sebastian_Vettel_2011_Malaysia_FP2_1.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/f/f7/Sebastian_Vettel_2011_Malaysia_FP2_1.jpg/440px-Sebastian_Vettel_2011_Malaysia_FP2_1.jpg 2x" data-file-width="2560" data-file-height="788" /></a>  <div class="thumbcaption"><div class="magnify"><a href="/wiki/File:Sebastian_Vettel_2011_Malaysia_FP2_1.jpg" class="internal" title="Enlarge"></a></div><a href="/wiki/Sebastian_Vettel" title="Sebastian Vettel">Sebastian Vettel</a> currently has four consecutive titles to his name, winning them all with <a href="/wiki/Red_Bull_Racing" title="Red Bull Racing">Red Bull Racing</a>.</div></div></div>\n<div class="thumb tright"><div class="thumbinner" style="width:222px;"><a href="/wiki/File:2017_British_Grand_Prix_(35895436386).jpg" class="image"><img alt="" //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/0/03/2017_British_Grand_Prix_%2835895436386%29.jpg/440px-2017_British_Grand_Prix_%2835895436386%29.jpg 2x" data-file-width="5760" data-file-height="3840" class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=List_of_Formula_One_World_Drivers%27_Champions&amp;action=edit&amp;section=6" title="Edit section: Note">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>\n<p>In <a href="/wiki/1966_Formula_One_season" title="1966 Formula One season">1966</a> Australian <a href="/wiki/Jack_Brabham" title="Jack Brabham">Jack Brabham</a> won the world championship driving <a href="/wiki/Brabham_BT19" title="Brabham BT19">his own car</a> powered by the Australian engine <a href="/wiki/Repco" title="Repco">Repco</a>, but the car was built by <a href="/wiki/Brabham" title="Brabham">his team</a> registered in Britain.<sup id="cite_ref-34" class="reference"><a
